###Martell History###
#####################
#Марон and Мирия have been put in, Daenerys has been made and connected to Nearys and Aegon the Unworthy plus Оливар. Martells now have Targ blood. :)
#I've put an equal number of female and male martells rulers. To simulate the absolute-cognatic succession.
#The first few would be Emperor tier Prince titles for the histories too. Until Марон, who'd be bumped down to King tier Prince.
###############################
###Unbowed, Unbent, Unbroken###
###############################
